<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Based on the spinbutton pattern</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports using the scroll wheel to increment and decrement the value</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Handles floating point rounding errors when incrementing, decrementing, and
snapping to step</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports pressing and holding the spin buttons to continuously increment or
decrement</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports rounding value to specific number of fraction digits</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports scrubbing interaction</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the number input correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the number input package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> numberInput</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/number-input&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The number input package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:number-input/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div <h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> to define the initial value. The value must be a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">string</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;13&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control the value externally.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Note:</strong> Since the value can be formatted, it&#x27;s important to preserve the
value as a string.</p>
</blockquote>

</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">    <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">      value <span class="token operator">=</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript"></span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="setting-a-minimum-and-maximum-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting a minimum and maximum value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-a-minimum-and-maximum-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">min</code> prop or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">max</code> prop to set an upper and lower limit for the input.
By default, the input will restrict the value to stay within the specified
range.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">min</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">max</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>To allow the value overflow the specified min or max, set the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowOverflow: true</code> in the context.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="validating-overflow-and-underflow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Validating overflow and underflow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#validating-overflow-and-underflow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueInvalid</code> to react when the value goes below <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">min</code> or above <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">max</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">min</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">max</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowOverflow</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueInvalid</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string, valueAsNumber: number, reason: &quot;rangeUnderflow&quot; | &quot;rangeOverflow&quot; }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">reason</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="scrubbing-the-input-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Scrubbing the input value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#scrubbing-the-input-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Number input supports the scrubber interaction pattern. To use this pattern,
spread <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getScrubberProps()</code> on the scrubbing element.</p>
<p>It uses the Pointer lock API and tracks the pointer movement. It also renders a
virtual cursor which mimics the real cursor&#x27;s pointer.</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:number-input/scrubber.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div <h3 id="using-the-mousewheel-to-change-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using the mousewheel to change value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-the-mousewheel-to-change-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The number input machine exposes a way to increment/decrement the value using
the mouse wheel event. To activate this, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowMouseWheel</code> property to
the machine&#x27;s context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowMouseWheel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="clamp-value-when-user-blurs-the-input" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Clamp value when user blurs the input<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#clamp-value-when-user-blurs-the-input"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>In most cases, users can type custom values in the input field. If the typed
value is greater than the max, the value is reset to max when the user blurs the
input.</p>
<p>To disable this behavior, pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clampValueOnBlur</code> and set to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">clampValueOnBlur</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-value-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for value changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-value-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the value changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string, valueAsNumber: number }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;value is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-value-commit" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for value commit<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-value-commit"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueCommit</code> to react when the value is committed (blur or Enter).</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueCommit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string, valueAsNumber: number }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;committed:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-focus-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for focus changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-focus-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code> to react to focus and blur transitions.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFocusChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { focused: boolean, value: string, valueAsNumber: number }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;focused:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">focused</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To use the number input within forms, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> property in the machine&#x27;s
context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;quantity&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="adjusting-the-precision-of-the-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Adjusting the precision of the value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#adjusting-the-precision-of-the-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To format the input value to be rounded to specific decimal points, set the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">formatOptions</code> and provide <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Intl.NumberFormatOptions</code> such as
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maximumFractionDigits</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minimumFractionDigits</code></p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">formatOptions</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">maximumFractionDigits</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">minimumFractionDigits</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-long-press-spin" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling long press spin<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-long-press-spin"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To disable the long press spin, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">spinOnPress</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">spinOnPress</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="choosing-mobile-keyboard-type" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Choosing mobile keyboard type<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#choosing-mobile-keyboard-type"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inputMode</code> to hint the keyboard type on mobile.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">inputMode</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;numeric&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;text&quot; | &quot;tel&quot; | &quot;numeric&quot; | &quot;decimal&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="format-and-parse-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Format and parse value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#format-and-parse-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To apply custom formatting to the input&#x27;s value, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">formatOptions</code> and
provide <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Intl.NumberFormatOptions</code> such as <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">style</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">currency</code></p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">formatOptions</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">style</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;currency&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">currency</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;USD&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize increment/decrement labels and value text.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">valueText</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>value<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> units</span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="submitting-with-an-external-form" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Submitting with an external form<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#submitting-with-an-external-form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code> if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM
subtree.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>numberInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;value&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">form</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;checkout-form&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the number input is disabled, the root, label and input parts will have
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute added to them.</p>
<p>The increment and decrement spin buttons are disabled when the number input is
disabled and the min/max is reached.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* disabled styles for the input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* disabled styles for the input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* disabled styles for the label */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;increment-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* disabled styles for the increment button */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;decrement-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* disabled styles for the decrement button */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The number input is invalid, either by passing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid: true</code> or when the value
exceeds the max and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowOverflow: true</code> is passed. When this happens, the
root, label and input parts will have <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code> attribute added to them.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* disabled styles for the input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* invalid styles for the input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* invalid styles for the label */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="readonly-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Readonly state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#readonly-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the number input is readonly, the input part will have <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-readonly</code>
added.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-readonly</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* readonly styles for the input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="increment-and-decrement-spin-buttons" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Increment and decrement spin buttons<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#increment-and-decrement-spin-buttons"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The spin buttons can be styled individually with their respective <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;increment-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The number input machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; label: string; input: string; incrementTrigger: string; decrementTrigger: string; scrubber: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the number input. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name attribute of the number input. class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 <h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The number input <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focused</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the input is focused.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the input is invalid.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">empty</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the input value is empty.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The formatted value of the input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">valueAsNumber</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The value of the input as a number.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em the value of the input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to clear the value of the input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold number input provides controls for editing, incrementing or decrementing\nnumeric values using the keyboard or pointer.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/number-input\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"NumberInput\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBased on the spinbutton pattern\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports using the scroll wheel to increment and decrement the value\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHandles floating point rounding errors when incrementing, decrementing, and\nsnapping to step\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports pressing and holding the spin buttons to continuously increment or\ndecrement\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports rounding value to specific number of fraction digits\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports scrubbing interaction\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the number input package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"number-input/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo set up the number input correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"number-input\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the number input package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as numberInput from \"@zag-js/number-input\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe number input package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"number-input/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e to define the initial value. The value must be a \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"13\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e to control the value externally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote:\u003c/strong\u003e Since the value can be formatted, it's important to preserve the\nvalue as a string.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"number-input/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting a minimum and maximum value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass the \u003ccode\u003emin\u003c/code\u003e prop or \u003ccode\u003emax\u003c/code\u003e prop to set an upper and lower limit for the input.\nBy default, the input will restrict the value to stay within the specified\nrange.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2,3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  min: 10,\n  max: 200,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo allow the value overflow the specified min or max, set the\n\u003ccode\u003eallowOverflow: true\u003c/code\u003e in the context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eValidating overflow and underflow\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonValueInvalid\u003c/code\u003e to react when the value goes below \u003ccode\u003emin\u003c/code\u003e or above \u003ccode\u003emax\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  min: 0,\n  max: 10,\n  allowOverflow: true,\n  onValueInvalid(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, valueAsNumber: number, reason: \"rangeUnderflow\" | \"rangeOverflow\" }\n    console.log(details.reason)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eScrubbing the input value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNumber input supports the scrubber interaction pattern. To use this pattern,\nspread \u003ccode\u003eapi.getScrubberProps()\u003c/code\u003e on the scrubbing element.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIt uses the Pointer lock API and tracks the pointer movement. It also renders a\nvirtual cursor which mimics the real cursor's pointer.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"number-input/scrubber.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsing the mousewheel to change value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe number input machine exposes a way to increment/decrement the value using\nthe mouse wheel event. To activate this, pass the \u003ccode\u003eallowMouseWheel\u003c/code\u003e property to\nthe machine's context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  allowMouseWheel: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClamp value when user blurs the input\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn most cases, users can type custom values in the input field. If the typed\nvalue is greater than the max, the value is reset to max when the user blurs the\ninput.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo disable this behavior, pass \u003ccode\u003eclampValueOnBlur\u003c/code\u003e and set to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  clampValueOnBlur: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for value changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the value changes, the \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is invoked.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, valueAsNumber: number }\n    console.log(\"value is:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for value commit\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonValueCommit\u003c/code\u003e to react when the value is committed (blur or Enter).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  onValueCommit(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, valueAsNumber: number }\n    console.log(\"committed:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for focus changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonFocusChange\u003c/code\u003e to react to focus and blur transitions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { focused: boolean, value: string, valueAsNumber: number }\n    console.log(\"focused:\", details.focused)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage within forms\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use the number input within forms, set the \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e property in the machine's\ncontext.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  name: \"quantity\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAdjusting the precision of the value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo format the input value to be rounded to specific decimal points, set the\n\u003ccode\u003eformatOptions\u003c/code\u003e and provide \u003ccode\u003eIntl.NumberFormatOptions\u003c/code\u003e such as\n\u003ccode\u003emaximumFractionDigits\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eminimumFractionDigits\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-5}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  formatOptions: {\n    maximumFractionDigits: 4,\n    minimumFractionDigits: 2,\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling long press spin\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo disable the long press spin, set the \u003ccode\u003espinOnPress\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  spinOnPress: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eChoosing mobile keyboard type\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003einputMode\u003c/code\u003e to hint the keyboard type on mobile.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  inputMode: \"numeric\", // \"text\" | \"tel\" | \"numeric\" | \"decimal\"\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eFormat and parse value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo apply custom formatting to the input's value, set the \u003ccode\u003eformatOptions\u003c/code\u003e and\nprovide \u003ccode\u003eIntl.NumberFormatOptions\u003c/code\u003e such as \u003ccode\u003estyle\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003ecurrency\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-5}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  formatOptions: {\n    style: \"currency\",\n    currency: \"USD\",\n likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T21bf,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"The number input provides controls for editing, incrementing or decrementing\nnumeric values using the keyboard or pointer.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/number-input\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"NumberInput\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Based on the spinbutton pattern\n- Supports using the scroll wheel to increment and decrement the value\n- Handles floating point rounding errors when incrementing, decrementing, and\n  snapping to step\n- Supports pressing and holding the spin buttons to continuously increment or\n  decrement\n- Supports rounding value to specific number of fraction digits\n- Supports scrubbing interaction\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the number input package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"number-input/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the number input correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"number-input\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the number input package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as numberInput from \"@zag-js/number-input\"\n```\n\nThe number input package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"number-input/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nSet `defaultValue` to define the initial value. The value must be a `string`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"13\",\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled value\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control the value externally.\n\n\u003e **Note:** Since the value can be formatted, it's important to preserve the\n\u003e value as a string.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"number-input/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting a minimum and maximum value\n\nPass the `min` prop or `max` prop to set an upper and lower limit for the input.\nBy default, the input will restrict the value to stay within the specified\nrange.\n\n```jsx {2,3}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  min: 10,\n  max: 200,\n})\n```\n\n\u003e To allow the value overflow the specified min or max, set the\n\u003e `allowOverflow: true` in the context.\n\n### Validating overflow and underflow\n\nUse `onValueInvalid` to react when the value goes below `min` or above `max`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  min: 0,\n  max: 10,\n  allowOverflow: true,\n  onValueInvalid(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, valueAsNumber: number, reason: \"rangeUnderflow\" | \"rangeOverflow\" }\n    console.log(details.reason)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Scrubbing the input value\n\nNumber input supports the scrubber interaction pattern. To use this pattern,\nspread `api.getScrubberProps()` on the scrubbing element.\n\nIt uses the Pointer lock API and tracks the pointer movement. It also renders a\nvirtual cursor which mimics the real cursor's pointer.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"number-input/scrubber.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Using the mousewheel to change value\n\nThe number input machine exposes a way to increment/decrement the value using\nthe mouse wheel event. To activate this, pass the `allowMouseWheel` property to\nthe machine's context.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  allowMouseWheel: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Clamp value when user blurs the input\n\nIn most cases, users can type custom values in the input field. If the typed\nvalue is greater than the max, the value is reset to max when the user blurs the\ninput.\n\nTo disable this behavior, pass `clampValueOnBlur` and set to `false`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  clampValueOnBlur: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for value changes\n\nWhen the value changes, the `onValueChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, valueAsNumber: number }\n    console.log(\"value is:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for value commit\n\nUse `onValueCommit` to react when the value is committed (blur or Enter).\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  onValueCommit(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, valueAsNumber: number }\n    console.log(\"committed:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for focus changes\n\nUse `onFocusChange` to react to focus and blur transitions.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { focused: boolean, value: string, valueAsNumber: number }\n    console.log(\"focused:\", details.focused)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nTo use the number input within forms, set the `name` property in the machine's\ncontext.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  name: \"quantity\",\n})\n```\n\n### Adjusting the precision of the value\n\nTo format the input value to be rounded to specific decimal points, set the\n`formatOptions` and provide `Intl.NumberFormatOptions` such as\n`maximumFractionDigits` or `minimumFractionDigits`\n\n```jsx {2-5}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  formatOptions: {\n    maximumFractionDigits: 4,\n    minimumFractionDigits: 2,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Disabling long press spin\n\nTo disable the long press spin, set the `spinOnPress` to `false`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  spinOnPress: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Choosing mobile keyboard type\n\nSet `inputMode` to hint the keyboard type on mobile.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  inputMode: \"numeric\", // \"text\" | \"tel\" | \"numeric\" | \"decimal\"\n})\n```\n\n### Format and parse value\n\nTo apply custom formatting to the input's value, set the `formatOptions` and\nprovide `Intl.NumberFormatOptions` such as `style` and `currency`\n\n```jsx {2-5}\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  formatOptions: {\n    style: \"currency\",\n    currency: \"USD\",\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing accessibility labels\n\nUse `translations` to customize increment/decrement labels and value text.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  translations: {\n    incrementLabel: \"Increase quantity\",\n    decrementLabel: \"Decrease quantity\",\n    valueText: (value) =\u003e `${value} units`,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Submitting with an external form\n\nSet `form` if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM\nsubtree.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(numberInput.machine, {\n  name: \"value\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Disabled state\n\nWhen the number input is disabled, the root, label and input parts will have\n`data-disabled` attribute added to them.\n\nThe increment and decrement spin buttons are disabled when the number input is\ndisabled and the min/max is reached.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* disabled styles for the input */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* disabled styles for the input */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* disabled styles for the label */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"increment-trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* disabled styles for the increment button */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"decrement-trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* disabled styles for the decrement button */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid state\n\nThe number input is invalid, either by passing `invalid: true` or when the value\nexceeds the max and `allowOverflow: true` is passed. When this happens, the\nroot, label and input parts will have `data-invalid` attribute added to them.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* disabled styles for the input */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* invalid styles for the input */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* invalid styles for the label */\n}\n```\n\n### Readonly state\n\nWhen the number input is readonly, the input part will have `data-readonly`\nadded.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-readonly] {\n  /* readonly styles for the input */\n}\n```\n\n### Increment and decrement spin buttons\n\nThe spin buttons can be styled individually with their respective `data-part`\nattribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"increment-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the increment trigger element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"decrement-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the decrement trigger element */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe number input machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"number-input\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe number input `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"number-input\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"number-input\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"number-input\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Number Input\",\"description\":\"Using the numeric input machine in your
